padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2323764" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Garylinnn"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2295236"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2295236.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Garylinnn" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2323764ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2323764" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2295236">Garylinnn</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-22"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1729610491" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The first time I encountered this perfume was when I was shopping at the department store. The salesperson handed me a fragrance strip with the dry down of Paradoxe. At first sniff, it was a very traditional sweet scent, with floral and fruity notes mixed with vanilla.<br />
Later, I decided to buy a 30ml bottle to try. The initial spray had a strong scent of bergamot mixed with honey and orange, which I found a bit overwhelming. It was very intense, and when I was studying in the morning, if I held my hand too close to my nose, I would have trouble breathing (so I sprayed a little less). After about two hours, I felt the scent had slightly faded.<br />
This fragrance lasts quite long, haha. I sprayed it in the morning and could still smell a faint scent in the evening. The transition between the top and base notes is not very obvious, it feels like the same scent all the time.<br />
After all, this is my personal opinion and feeling about this perfume. It's really sweet, suitable for girls who like sweet scents. As a guy, I wouldn't wear it, but it's quite suitable to spray on clothes.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="75668"comment_id="2323764"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-Paradoxe-75668.html?ccid=2323764#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2321833" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; She tried it at a department store then ordered it on line. It is a floral scent, it opens clean fresh, goes into floral with this weird note(thinking animalic jasmin) just behind the florals not a nice note. Then the sweetness comes in but florals still very present, the weird note tones down.<br />
 It doesn’t project more than an hour, and becomes a skin scent after around 6 hour but lasts on skin like 12hrs. I personally did not like it, it immediately reminded me of scented trash bags or like restroom deodorizing spray. <br />
It is for a more mature audience, not very casual. It is an everyday work setting but it still can be used for an event. Applications 2-4 max as the opening and first hour can be a little too much. Once it dries down it stays closer to you. <br />
She has worn miss Dior absolutely blooming for years straight(my favorite when she wears it). In the past she got alien but she only wore it a couple of times and gave the bottle to my oldest daughter. Got black opium also gave it to my daughter. A Guerlain bloom of rose edt; same thing ended up with my daughter. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1596404">Threadg0ld</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-03">09/03/24 05:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My sig frag since 2005 when I got married has been Prada Prada (sometimes I think called Prada Amber). And as usual when I find a perfume I adore, it has become discontinued. I've been keeping an eye (or a nose?) out for a new signature fragrance. I had smelt Paradox via one of those little slippery foil samples that came with Vogue magazine but it didn't speak to me at all, I thought it was just like all the recent perfumes, a bit bland, a bit generic, harmless, not striking. So, when I received a present of Paradox 2 weeks ago, I must admit I was glad of a nice gift but not too enthused (am I horrible?). But from the first day I wore it. WOW! I love it. So warm, so cozy, enticing, embracing, a little sexy but not dirty sexy. Quite sweet and caramelish which I don't usually like but this time I do. Quite Christmassy but still suitable for all year round. I look forward to getting a gift coffret of this for a Christmas gift actually. I still really love Prada Prada but this is a very able replacement. Everywhere I go wearing Paradox, I get compliments, even from strangers who stop me to ask what my perfume is. It just goes to show how useless those little magazine perfume samples are. If you are considering a fragrance, it really is worth getting a spray on the skin in the department store and seeing how you feel all day with it. <br />
Footnote - I bought Ungaro (2007) this week and find it very similar to Paradox, same warmth, same amber.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="75668"comment_id="2269939"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-Paradoxe-75668.html?ccid=2269939#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2269101" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2212076" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="scentine"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1210646"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1210646.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="scentine" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2212076ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2212076" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1210646">scentine</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-08">07/08/24 12:55</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I stand corrected. I've done a complete 180 on this, to my own great surprise. When it came out I immediately wrote this off as unpalatably generic. It seemed like another drop in a sea of uninspired releases. Everything has 289 flankers now, that you can't tell apart. There are few good surprises among the many indistinguishable disappointments.<br />
This is how I felt about it, initially. But somehow I have come around and started picking up on this among everything else. It is possible that my own changing tastes have warmed to it, but I think the most paradoxical thing about this is that despite its similarity to so many things, despite its sweetness, despite its apparent lack of individualism it has somehow become intoxicating. It is just alluring and pleasant and makes me want to breathe it in. Perhaps that is really what it is. Objectively it could bore us to death at this point, but somehow I seem to be fine with it and feel elated when I catch wafts of it coming off my hair and clothes.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2194855" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="julzvangogh"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2033828"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2033828.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="julzvangogh" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Prada/Prada-Paradoxe-75668.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.75668.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Prada Paradoxe"title="Prada Paradoxe"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2194855ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2194855" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2033828">julzvangogh</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-21">06/21/24 01:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I saw a lot of reviews calling the perfume outdated, generic, boring or cheap. I heavily disagree. I got this perfume as a gift and I was skeptical at first, influenced by the comments, thinking it would be too mainstream. <br />
<br />
But now, roughly 1 1/2 months later, it's my to-go, everyday/ every situation kind of scent. Its notes are delicious, feminine, mature, and fresh. It's appropriate for professional or private occasions, suitable for day and night. It leaves a trail on my clothes for a long time, and I can just smell it all the time without being overwhelmed by the scent, getting a headache or nausea. <br />
<br />
Sure, it's probably the wrong scent if you're looking for something totally unique, but I can definitely recommend to add for your daily collection. Once my bottle is used I will definitely get another one!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="75668"comment_id="2194855"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-Paradoxe-75668.html?ccid=2194855#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2192453" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It has a musty, dusty base and moldy basement dry-down. <br />
<br />
Givenchy Amarige (zero moldy note) or Tresor (somewhat moldy note) by lancome have similar DNA without the heavy moldy funk and better cost/value ratio. <br />
<br />
This also reminds me of bodycology pink vanilla wish with the suffocating melted waxy plastic vanilla base. <br />
<br />
I would not pay hundreds for this, let alone wear it proving just because a scent is created by a luxury brand does not mean you will like it or there will be hits and misses with every brand or fragrance house.  <br />
<br />
Buy and wear what you like and what smells good to you.  Do not worry about the brand unless its for display purposes only.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="75668"comment_id="2146000"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-Paradoxe-75668.html?ccid=2146000#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2141446" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1173739">laurelin08</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-24">03/24/24 17:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I originally tested this last May and for whatever reason passed it up, but I recently revisited this on a cruise and I became enamored. I sprayed some on my wrist in the evening and I woke up still smelling it's beautiful scent. I've only come across a handful of scents that are that long lasting. I bought it 2 weeks later when I just couldn't stop thinking about it, also there was a massive discount on Amazon, Yay! It's warm, but also fresh. It's sweet, but not gourmand. It's citrusy and clean, but never screechy. It's youthful and mature. In this way, it does remind me of Flowerbomb in that it's simultaneously warm and fresh. Honestly, I could see it as being a crowd pleaser and that's actually a good thing because the quality of the perfume is exceptional. It's blended oh so beautifully. My husband says it's smells interesting and fun and kind of like Pez candy, which I can understand. It does have an addictive play-doh type smell similar to Dior Poison Girl, but without the spice. I love that warm and sweet smell!<br />
<br />
This perfume is a paradox in itself as it smells distinctive yet like an amalgamation of other perfumes I've worn such as Ellie Saab Le Parfum, Ellie Saab in White, My Way Parfum, Armani Code, and Poison Girl. It has to be the orange blossom, orange, and vanilla combination that connect all these scents together especially the orange blossom. Prada Paradoxe, while reminding me of many other perfumes, still smells unique and special, its more versatile than all the previously mentioned fragrances meaning that it can be worn for any season and any occasion. I wore it to work the other day and its gorgeous scent was gently wafting at me all day long.  Because of this and its powerhouse strength, Prada Pardoxe is signature fragrance worthy. It's definitely become a staple in my fragrance wardrobe.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="75668"comment_id="2103040"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-Paradoxe-75668.html?ccid=2103040#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2100177" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Soft and POWDERY. If I want a little more kick, I layer with Goddess/Voce Viva. If I want to sweeten it up, I wear with Born in Roma. It's safe for "basic" noses like myself but also unique enough that I think niche folks can enjoy. Surprisingly strong and long lasting!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="75668"comment_id="2088233"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-Paradoxe-75668.html?ccid=2088233#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2087151" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1764842">cintara4999</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-01">03/01/24 23:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I really like this fragrance. Is it simple? Yes. Is it generic? Yes. But is it lovely? Also yes. <br />
This is probable what most people think of when you say “perfume”. A little bit sweet, a little bit floral, with hints of citrus. Though on my skin it opens up with mostly white flowers. The scent is really nothing special but I don’t think of it as a bad thing. I used my sample whenever I wanted to smell girly, fresh and flirty. What actually surprised me was the longevity. On my skin the base notes were still present after about 12 hours. On clothes it stays for days. I will probably buy a whole bottle mainly because of how long-lasting it is.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="75668"comment_id="2079552"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-Paradoxe-75668.html?ccid=2079552#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2076379" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2076379" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="AbiSmellsDelish"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2036210"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="AbiSmellsDelish" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2076379ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2076379" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2036210">AbiSmellsDelish</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-27">02/27/24 22:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I LOVE this scent. My ex husband gifted it to me for Christmas. He mentioned it reminded him of YSL Libre which I own and love. <br />
At first I rolled my eyes at the thought I would be wearing the same scent as most girls a decade younger than me. <br />
Once I tried it I truly have not been able to stop using it! <br />
First, it’s very much a gourmand scent to me. It’s very sweet, very intense (in a good way), almost reminds me of a grape scent. Very reminiscent of the fresh grape scent in Victoria’s Secret’s Body Rush Grapesicle. This may be the neroli and orange blossom mix. <br />
This scent lasts for DAYS! There are times I spray it on my clothes and can smell it days later. <br />
There is literally no reason to walk around with a travel size of this scent. <br />
It’s intensity matches that of YSL Libre, YSL Black Opium, and Thierry Mugler Alien.<br />
I wouldn’t say this is an exclusively night or winter scent as I can see this working for a Spring evening, girls night or date night. <br />
It’s still very youthful in a sense, as I only know of women in their early 20s going bonkers for this scent.<br />
It’s sweet but I don’t get florals other than the orange blossom. Nor do I get powdery in any sense. If it’s there it’s very subtle. There is vanilla present for sure as I notice it towards the end of my day. <br />
If you love gourmands and need something more youthful than YSL Libre, this is safe bet.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="75668"comment_id="2076379"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-Paradoxe-75668.html?ccid=2076379#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2076298" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's a good balance of floral, fruity and sweet with a soft muskiness. It's distinctive from the others. Sometimes I go to sephora and spray tons of paper samples. After a few minutes for many I can't tell which is which for most of them. But Paradox has a distinct tartness to it so I can always recognize it. It's fun and feminine and likeable. I think of it is the same category as Donna Born in Roma. That one is less tart and more floral and the dry down is more spicy. I prefer Paradox. I think it can work for everyday but also for going out. I can understand why some people might think it isn't interesting enough. I'm on the fence if it feels like me and whether I would want to purchase a bottle. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1346348">vulgarsaint</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-08-14">08/14/22 13:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>oh boy, i really had my hopes up for this one. <br />
it was very exciting to see prada coming up with something other than another candy flanker. i was happy to get my hands on a sample so early on and i couldn’t wait for it to arrive.<br />
and well, i lasted less than an hour with this on my wrist.<br />
if you’re into perfumery you can already see, based on the notes, that this isn’t going to be anything special. and it is not. i personally like to be able to recognise perfume by just the scent, that’s what makes it a good perfume in my opinion. but this, i feel like i’ve smelt this so many times already. neroli, orange blossom and vanilla? groundbreaking. but that wasn’t even my biggest issue.<br />
and my biggest issue was that this is just too much for me. something about the sweetness and the fruity note combined with how musky it is at the same time is so incredibly nauseating to me. quite literally, because it triggered my migraine. <br />
if you’re a fan of prada, both as a fashion house and based on previous perfumes, this just doesn’t fit the vibe. everything from the scent to the bottle appears, to my nose and eyes, for the lack of the better word cheap. if i didn’t know better i’d be convinced this is a random knockoff of a perfume that doesn’t even exist, just with the brand name slapped on it.<br />
<br />
(because i’ve gotten very angry private messages in response to negative reviews before, a perfume review is always going to be very subjective. this is how i perceive it. you might love it and that’s okay. don’t send me death threats please lol)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="75668"comment_id="1623622"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-Paradoxe-75668.html?ccid=1623622#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1633588" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1633588" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="korrocks"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1058646"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1058646.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="korrocks" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Narciso-Rodriguez/Narciso-Eau-de-Toilette-30658.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.30658.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Narciso Eau de Toilette"title="Narciso Eau de Toilette"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1633588ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1633588" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1058646">korrocks</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-08-29">08/29/22 07:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A truly terrible trend has cropped up in recent years, one I hopped wouldn't catch on and has instead spread like wildfire.<br />
<br />
Here's the recipe: take the suffocating coffee-and-almond-syrup base of Black Opium and its congeners, mix it with some harsh, sugary white floral notes of orange blossom and tuberose, and send it roiling into the atmosphere in a cute bottle.<br />
<br />
It worked for So Scandal, My Way, L'Interdit and Woman (Ralph Lauren), and it's probably going to work for Prada. I imagine the Paradoxe in question is how this once trendsetting fashion house is now following what everyone else is doing.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="75668"comment_id="1633588"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-Paradoxe-75668.html?ccid=1633588#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1651288" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
To smell like an industrial cake in plastic-wrapped portions is not and will never be sexy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="75668"comment_id="1636737"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Prada/Prada-Paradoxe-75668.html?ccid=1636737#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="75668" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
